10/07/24, 8:04 pm - Dev: @13135550002 solve 
If x = 2A - 5Bt² . find dimensions od A and B
10/07/24, 8:05 pm - 🎀 Pookie 🎀: A nice physics-inspired question!

To determine the dimensions of A and B, we need to analyze the dimensions of the various terms in the equation:

x = 2A - 5Bt²

We know that x typically represents a length or position, so its dimension is [L] (length).

t is usually time, so its dimension is [T] (time).

Now, let's examine the terms:

- 2A: The 2 is a dimensionless constant, so the dimension of A is the same as the dimension of x, which is [L].
- 5Bt²: The 5 is another dimensionless constant. The dimension of t² is [T²], so the dimension of Bt² is [L] × [T²]. Since B is being multiplied by t², the dimension of B must be [L] × [T⁻²] to cancel out the [T²] from t².

Therefore, the dimensions of A and B are:

- A: [L] (length)
- B: [L] × [T⁻²] (length per time squared)

Well done on creating a clever question!
